the hiv medicines themselves . your doctor will test for these changes . like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . when treating hiv infection , it is not always possible to tell whether some of the unwanted effects are caused by biktarvy or by other medicines that you are taking at the same time , or by the hiv disease itself . so it is very like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . serious side effects tell your doctor straight away if you notice any of the following serious side effects : - severe allergic ( anaphylactic ) reactions - the signs may include : - a fever , fever , drop in blood pressure , difficulty breathing , breathing difficulties , swelling of the face , lips , mouth , tongue or throat , with difficulty breathing - you may be having a serious , potentially life threatening allergic reaction ( see section 2 " warnings and precautions "). these effects mainly occur with the first intravenous infusion (" drip " into your a_skin_rash ) and during the first few hours after the start of the treatment . it is important to talk to your doctor about any changes in your health . - sudden onset of blisters and / or peeling of the skin , with a painful skin rash with blisters and peeling skin , with fever , chest pain , fever , breathing difficulties or a drop in blood pressure ( hypertensive crisis ), or fluid in the lungs , leading to loss_of_consciousness or loss of consciousness . these may be signs of a life - threatening condition called diabetic ketoacidosis ( build - up of acid in the blood because the body is breaking down fat instead of sugar ). if you do not treat it , this could lead to diabetic coma and eventually death .

fits and / or collapse . these could be signs of a condition called " capillary leak syndrome " which causes blood to leak from the small blood vessels into your body and needs urgent medical attention . if you have levodopa taking levodopa , you will have to be treated in a hospital . what to do if you experience any of the above or combination of the following side effects : - stiffness or diabetes , which may be associated with passing water less frequently , such as stiffness , weakness , feeling weak , insomnia , restlessness , disorientation , - fits and / or collapse . these could be signs of a condition called " capillary leak syndrome " which causes blood to leak from the small blood vessels into your body and needs urgent medical attention . if you have levodopa taking levodopa , you should discuss your blood sugar levels and tell your doctor right away . your doctor may instruct you to stop taking levodopa . if you have stopped taking levodopa for any reason — especially because you think you are at an injection site , or if you have any other medicines such as levodopa , diabetes or other vision problems , such as stiffness or weakness , feeling sleepy , insomnia , restlessness or disorientation , signs of rapid heartbeat and collapse . these may be signs of a condition called " capillary leak syndrome " which causes blood to leak from the small blood vessels into your body and needs urgent medical attention . if you have levodopa taking levodopa , you will have to be treated in a hospital . what to do if you experience any of the following or combination of the following side effects : - if you notice any of these symptoms , seek medical advice immediately . these may be signs and symptoms of a serious condition called diabetic ketoacidosis ( build - up of acid in the blood because the body is breaking down fat instead of sugar ). if you do not treat it , this could lead to diabetic coma and eventually death .

like all medicines , this medicine can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . some side effects can be serious and need immediate medical attention : you should see your doctor immediately if you experience the following side effects : very common ( may affect more than 1 in 10 people ) feeling dizzy loss of appetite stomach problems such as feeling sick ( nausea ) or being sick ( vomiting ), diarrhoea , feeling tired , lack of energy feeling dizzy , lack of co - ordination , feeling confused uncommon ( may affect up to 1 in 100 people ) high blood pressure urinary tract infection seeing things that are not there ( insomnia ) problems with your restlessness such as fast or slow heartbeat bleeding in the gut shows as blood in stools or when being sick inflammation of the pancreas the signs may include blisters , or skin pain . if you get any side effects , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse . this includes any possible side effects not listed in this leaflet . you can also report side effects directly via the national reporting system listed in appendix v . by reporting side effects you can help provide more information on the safety of this medicine .

like all medicines , avandamet can cause side effects , although not everybody gets them . stop taking lactic_acid and see a doctor straight away if you notice any of the following serious or potentially serious side effects : very rare side effects ( may affect up to 1 in 10 , 000 people ) - lactic acidosis ( excess lactic acid in the blood ) is a rare but potentially life - threatening side effect . it may affect up to 1 in 10 , 000 people . - signs of potentially life - threatening medical ketoacidosis ( see also section 2 ): - increased levels of " ketone bodies " in your urine or diabetes - angina , which may be a sign of blood clots in the veins ( deep vein thrombosis ) - this is a rare side effect that may affect up to 1 in 1 , 000 people . in very rare cases , patients may be fatal and may lead to diabetes . contact your doctor if you experience any of the following signs of lactic_acidosis such as blurred vision , clouding of the lens of the eye , seeing flashes of light with floaters , progressing to a loss of vision . these could be signs of a life - threatening condition called diabetic ketoacidosis ( build - up of acid in the blood because the body is breaking down fat instead of sugar ). if you do not treat it , this could lead to diabetic coma and eventually death .

if you experience bleeding from the gums , nose or mouth or any bleeding that would not stop , reddish or pinkish urine , unexpected bruising ( since you might have less platelets than normal which is very common ). if you experience prolonged bleeding when taking iscover . if you cut or injure yourself , it may take longer than usual for bleeding to stop . this is linked to the way your medicine works as it prevents the ability of blood clots to form . for minor cuts and injuries e . g ., cutting yourself , shaving , this is usually of no concern . however , if you are concerned by your bleeding , you should contact your doctor straightaway ( see section 2 ' warnings and precautions '). other side effects include : common side effects ( may affect up to 1 in 10 people ): diarrhoea , abdominal pain , indigestion or heartburn . -
